msg:Very good experienceÔøº, Ye Chen at the front desk was very attentive and made great arrangementsÔøº

The overall architectural style of Yihai Town is designed based on the classical style of a small town in southern France. Both the exterior and the guest rooms are full of exotic style. Walking into it feels like traveling into a fairy tale. Yihai Town has received widespread expectations from all walks of life before its opening with its unique European-style architecture and French country-style park.

Yihai Town consists of five inns: "Aris Inn", "Susuli Inn", "Migen Inn", "Oli Inn" and "Tuosuo Inn", with a total of 56 rooms and a courtyard. Suites, parent-child rooms and sea view rooms. Looking out from the guest room window, you can have a panoramic view of the blue sea. The interior design adopts French modern fashion style, with the four seasons as the theme, presenting four different types of exquisite interior designs. Various modern artworks can be seen everywhere in the corridors and guest rooms. It is an ingenious work carefully created by Tefang Group, which combines simplicity and elegance, and the intersection of art and humanity.
